                                            SUBWAY ENVIRONMENT SIMULATION
                                                  SIMULATION OF
                         SES v4.1 file for illustrating the losses upwind and downwind of fires.
                         This file has three line segments.  The first segment has a a jet fan,
                         the second segment has a fire and the third segment is downwind of the fire.
                         In this run, a loss is applied at the forward end of the second segment.
                         The correction for density uses the temperature at the forward end of the
                         second segment.
